    <h3 class="Fw-b Fz-l Mb-2 Lh-12 Ov-h" style="max-height:4.667em">
        <a href="https://ca.news.yahoo.com/woman-23-begs-die-insect-155923130.html"   data-ylk="cpos:14;bpos:1;cat:default;t1:a3;t2:strm;t3:ct;g:e5208f99-5791-36e3-97d4-9d4c5e981c3c;ct:1;pkgt:5;elm:hdln;elmt:ct;rspns:nav;itc:0;r:P0f00000000;ccode:mdsfb;" class="js-stream-content-link Mend-4">Woman, 23, Begs To Die After Insect Bite Leaves Her Bed-Ridden For 11 Years</a>
    </h3>
    <p class="Mb-2 LineClamp-3">A 23-year-old woman who has been bed-ridden for 11 years has told her family she wants to die in a suicide assisted clinic in Switzerland. Kirsty Keep contracted lupus after she was bitten by a bug in her back garden in Maidstone, Kent when she was 12 years old. Kirsty also started having seizures 18 months ago.</p>

        <a href="https://ca.news.yahoo.com/story-behind-10-famous-doctored-162819728.html"   data-ylk="cpos:17;bpos:1;cat:default;t1:a3;t2:strm;t3:ct;g:d1e822a2-c5c5-3095-832d-61c4f6fa4b9d;ct:1;pkgt:4;elm:hdln;elmt:ct;rspns:nav;itc:0;r:P0f00000000;ccode:mdsfb;" class="js-stream-content-link Mend-4">The Story Behind 10 Infamous Doctored Photos</a>
    </h3>
    
    <p class="Mb-2">Image manipulation may feel like a modern invention, but the practice has existed for as long as photography itself. A good place to start is with what could be the world’s first ‘Photoshop’ job – an iconic image of a statesmanlike Abraham Lincoln (above main), which turned out, in fact, to be two separate photographs. “Stalin, Mao, Hitler, Mussolini, Castro, Brezhnev, and many others had photographs manipulated in an attempt to rewrite history,” says Dr Hany Farid of image forensics company FourAndSix.</p>

        <a href="https://ca.news.yahoo.com/planet-nine-nasas-saturn-probe-helps-hunt-122255376.html"   data-ylk="cpos:19;bpos:1;cat:default;t1:a3;t2:strm;t3:ct;g:8037804d-1fbe-3088-9f7a-2ed350f66492;ct:1;pkgt:4;elm:hdln;elmt:ct;rspns:nav;itc:0;r:P0f00000000;ccode:mdsfb;" class="js-stream-content-link Mend-4">Find Planet Nine! NASA&#39;s Saturn Probe Helps with the Hunt</a>
    </h3>
    
    <p class="Mb-2">The search for a possible ninth planet, far beyond the orbit of Pluto, is being assisted by NASA&#39;s Cassini probe, which has been exploring the Saturn system for more than a decade. The news that a possible ninth planet with a mass 10 times that of Earth could be orbiting in the dark region beyond Neptune lit up the public&#39;s imagination in January. The work relies heavily on measurements taken by the Cassini probe, and aims to narrow down the hunting zone where scientists should point their telescopes as they search for this hidden monster.</p>
